<strong>colloid</strong><div style="margin-bottom:20px;"><div><span style="padding-left:10px;"><strong></strong></span></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">A mixture in which very small particles of one substance are distributed evenly throughout another substance. The particles are generally larger than those in a solution, and smaller than those in a suspension. Paints, milk, and fog are colloids. Compare  solution suspension.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:20px;"><div><span style="padding-left:10px;"><strong>adj.</strong></span></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">Of, relating to, containing, or having the nature of a colloid.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:20px;"><div><span style="padding-left:10px;"><strong>adjective</strong></span></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">Relating to or characterized by a colloid or colloids.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px"> Physical Chemistry. <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">pathol <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">of, denoting, or having the character of a colloid<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:20px;"><div><span style="padding-left:10px;"><strong>n.</strong></span></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">A suspension of finely divided particles in a continuous medium from which the particles do not settle out rapidly and are not readily filtered.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">The particulate matter so suspended.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">The gelatinous stored secretion of the thyroid gland, consisting mainly of thyroglobulin.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">Gelatinous material resulting from colloid degeneration in diseased tissue.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:20px;"><div><span style="padding-left:10px;"><strong>noun</strong></span></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">A homogeneous non-crystalline substance consisting of large molecules or ultramicroscopic particles of one substance dispersed through a second substance. Colloids include gels, sols, and emulsions; the particles do not settle, and cannot be separated out by ordinary filtering or centrifuging like those in a suspension.<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px"> Physical Chemistry. <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px"> Medicine/Medical. <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">Also called: colloidal solution, colloidal suspension <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">the solid suspended phase in such a mixture<div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">obsolete <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div><div style="padding-left:20px;padding-right:20px; margin-bottom: 8px">physiol <div style="padding-left:15px;color:#545454"></div></div></div>
